Source Code

These source-code files were from the printout at the MIT Museum, with many thanks to Deborah Douglas, the Museum's Curator of Science and Technology, for releasing it to us. The printout was digitally photographed by Paul Fjeld. A team of volunteers transcribed the source code manually from these images or, where appropriate, modified already-transcribed but similar source Colossus 249 (Apollo 9) source code to agree with the images from the printout. Note that the page images presented online are of reduced quality, and that higher-quality images are available. Report any conversion errors or legibility problems in page images to info@sandroid.org. Notations on the program listing read, in part:

	GAP:  ASSEMBLE REVISION 055 OF AGC PROGRAM COMANCHE BY NASA 2021113-051
	10:28 APR.  1,1969
Note that the date is the date of the printout, not the date of the program revision. 

000002,000002:                                                                                                  #  Copyright:    Public domain.
000003,000003:                                                                                                  #  Filename:     MAIN.agc
000004,000004:                                                                                                  #  Purpose:      Part of the source code for Colossus 2A, AKA Comanche 055.
000005,000005:                                                                                                  #                It is part of the source code for the Command Module's (CM)
000006,000006:                                                                                                  #                Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC) Apollo 11.
000007,000007:                                                                                                  #  Assembler:    yaYUL
000008,000008:                                                                                                  #  Contact:      Ron Burkey <info@sandroid.org>.
000009,000009:                                                                                                  #  Website:      www.ibiblio.org/apollo
000010,000010:                                                                                                  #  Mod history:  2009-05-05 RSB  Adapted from Colossus249/MAIN.agc.
000011,000011: 
000012,000012:                                                                                                  #  This source code has been transcribed or otherwise adapted from digitized
000013,000013:                                                                                                  #  images of a hardcopy from the MIT Museum.  The digitization was performed
000014,000014:                                                                                                  #  by Paul Fjeld, and arranged for by Deborah Douglas of the Museum.  Many
000015,000015:                                                                                                  #  thanks to both.  The images (with suitable reduction in storage size and
000016,000016:                                                                                                  #  consequent reduction in image quality as well) are available online at
000017,000017:                                                                                                  #  www.ibiblio.org/apollo.  If for some reason you find that the images are
000018,000018:                                                                                                  #  illegible, contact me at info@sandroid.org about getting access to the 
000019,000019:                                                                                                  #  (much) higher-quality images which Paul actually created.
000020,000020: 
000021,000021:                                                                                                  #  Notations on the hardcopy document read, in part:
000022,000022: 
000023,000023:                                                                                                  #        Assemble revision 055 of AGC program Comanche by NASA
000024,000024:                                                                                                  #        2021113-051.  10:28 APR. 1, 1969  
000025,000025: 
000026,000026:                                                                                                  #        This AGC program shall also be referred to as
000027,000027:                                                                                                  #                        Colossus 2A
000028,000028: 
000029,000029:                                                                                                  #  This file is a little different from the other Comanche055 files I'm providing, 
000030,000030:                                                                                                  #  in that it doesn't represent anything that appears directly in the original source.  
000031,000031:                                                                                                  #  What I (RSB) have done for organizational purposes is to split the huge monolithic
000032,000032:                                                                                                  #  source code into smaller, more manageable chunks--i.e., into individual source 
000033,000033:                                                                                                  #  files.  Those files are rejoined within this file as "includes".  It just makes
000034,000034:                                                                                                  #  it a little easier to work with.  The code chunks correspond to natural divisions
000035,000035:                                                                                                  #  into sub-programs.  In fact, these divisions are more-or-less specified by
000036,000036:                                                                                                  #  the source code itself.  Refer to the "SUBROUTINE CALLS" at the
000037,000037:                                                                                                  #  very beginning of the file ASSEMBLY_AND_OPERATION_INFORMATION.agc.
000038,000038: 
000039,000039:                                                                                                  #  It may be reasonably asked why tens of thousands of lines of source are joined by
000040,000040:                                                                                                  #  means of inclusion, rather than simply assembling the source files individually and
000041,000041:                                                                                                  #  then linking them to form the executable.  The answer is that the original 
000042,000042:                                                                                                  #  development team had no linker.  The builds were monolithic just like this.
000043,000043:                                                                                                  #  There was a big emphasis on reusability of the code in the original project, 
000044,000044:                                                                                                  #  apparently, but this reusability took the form of inserting your deck of 
000045,000045:                                                                                                  #  punch-cards at the appropriate position in somebody else's deck of punch-cards.
000046,000046:                                                                                                  #  (Actually, I think the card-decks were turned into tape libraries, and the modules
000047,000047:                                                                                                  #  were mixed-and-matched from the tape libraries, but the principle is the same.)
000048,000048:                                                                                                  #  So, indeed, the method of file-inclusion is a very fair representation of the 
000049,000049:                                                                                                  #  methods used in the original development ... with the improvement, of course,
000050,000050:                                                                                                  #  that you no longer have to worry about dropping the card deck.  On the other hand, 
000051,000051:                                                                                                  #  I wasn't there at the time, so I may have no idea what I'm talking about.
000052,000052: 
000053,000053:                                                                                                  #  Finally, note that the original Apollo AGC assembler (called "YUL") is no longer 
000054,000054:                                                                                                  #  available (as far as I can tell).  Actually, it had already been replaced by another
000055,000055:                                                                                                  #  assembler (called "GAP") by the time of Apollo 11, but GAP isn't available either.
000056,000056:                                                                                                  #  The replacement assembler yaYUL accepts a slightly different format for the source 
000057,000057:                                                                                                  #  code from what YUL or GAP accepted, so the source code has been targeted for 
000058,000058:                                                                                                  #  assembly with yaYUL.
000059,000059: 
000060,000060:                                                                                                  #  What follows is simply a bunch of file-includes for the individual code chunks.
000061,000061:                                                                                                  #  I've marked the page numbers to make proof-reading easier.  The page images also
000062,000062:                                                                                                  #  contain a lot of interesting tables (cross-referenced to page numbers) created by GAP, 
000063,000063:                                                                                                  #  but not duplicated by yaYUL, so it's still valuable even if the source-files
000064,000064:                                                                                                  #  listed below are in hand.
